 There is a lot of politics and debate on this
 aisa kaha ja rahaa he ki assam enarasi ke maamle main pahal karne vaala pehla rajya he or ab baaki rajyon main bhi enarasi laane kii maang kii ja rahi he
 But you will be surprised to know that NRC has already been prepared in all the states of the country
 aaie jaanate hai kya he sachai
 
 
 In fact, after the partition of the country, it was necessary to know how many people have been in the country legitimately or illegally
 isliye aazaadee ke baad saal 1951 main hi desh bhar main ek neshnal register of citigens taiyaar kiya gaya tha
 It was formulated in all states
 is tarah abhi assam main jo enarasi taiyaar kiya ja rahaa he vah nayaa nahin he, balki 1951 ke enarasi ko hi apadet kiya ja rahaa he
 In the year 1951, a nationwide census was conducted, in which information was obtained according to the order of all the houses in each village and how many people live in it
 iske baad is janaganana kii sahaayta se hi neshnal register of citigens taiyaar kiya gaya
 After preparing this register, it was placed in the offices of deputy commissioner and SDM of all areas on the instructions of the central government
 baad main 1960 ke dashak main ye register police vibhaag ko saunp die gaye
 What is the NRC of Assam: The NRC of Assam is actually an exercise to update the NRC formed in the year 1951
 isamen un sabhi logon ko shaamil kiya ja rahaa he jinka naam 1971 se pehle kii matadaata suchi yaa 1951 ke enarasi main shaamil he
 How NRC was updated in Assam The fact that the NRC was prepared in 1951 in all the states was based on the census, in which proper verification of people was not done
 is tarah assam main enarasi kaa apadation, vah bhi citigenship ke veriphication ke saath karne kii itani badi kavayad kisi rajya main pehali baar hui he
 In the 1980s, there was a major movement to eject illegal people in Assam
 ol assam students unionne pradhanmantri ko gyaapan dekar 1951 ke enarasi ko apadet karne kii maang kii
 But after this, the Assam Accord signed in 1985 did not include the update of NRC
 1990 main aasu ne maang kii ki assam samjhaute ko lagu kiya jaae
 It was then decided to update the NRC in the tripartite agreement on 17 November 1999
 manmohan singh ke daur main mili manzooritatkaleen sarkaar ne shuruaati kaam ke liye 20 karod rupee kii raashi manjuur kii
 But for many reasons this work could not be started
 iske baad phir manmohan singh ke kaarykaal main 5 may, 2005 main hue tripaksheeya samjhaute main enarasi ko apadet karne karne ko manjuuri mili
 But the work did not progress much further
 phir 22 april, 2010 ko hui ek tripaksheeya baithak ke baad rajya ke chigaanv or barpeta cirkil main payalat project shuru hua
 The UPA government gave the responsibility to Prateik Hajela The current process started with the UPA government itself in 2013, when Prateek Hajela was upgraded to NRC and made the State Coordinator
 lekin vaastavik kaary ne teji pakadi farvari 2015 main jab enarasi seva kendron ko sthapit karne kii prakriya shuru hui or 6
 3 to put names in NRC with 6 crore documents
 29 karod logon ne applai kiya
 Supreme Court directive In August 2014, the Supreme Court ordered the Assam government to complete the entire NRC updation process within three years
 centre sarkaar ne is register ko apadet karne ke liye 288 karod rupee manjuur kiye

 rahul gandhi ke congress kaa kaman sanbhale abhi ek hi haftaa hua he, lekin itane kam samay main bhi unki leadership ne party ko kam se kam 3 maukon par 'achche din' hi dikhaa diya
 On December 16, Rahul took charge of the Congress after 19 years of Sonia Gandhi
 sonia gandhi ke kaarykaal main desh kii sabase puraani party 10 saal satta main rahi, lekin pichley 3 saalon main party ke liye kuch bhi acha nahin ho rahaa tha or na sirf centre main uski sthiti behad kharaab hui balki ek-ek karke rajyon se uski satta jaati rahi
 Today the situation is that the Congress is in power in only 4 states
 rahul ne gujarat chunaav ke dauraan hi congress kii kaman sanbhali or aakraamak andaaj main prachaar karte hue khud ko ek shashakt netaa ke rup main pesh kiya
 Before the Gujarat elections, he was considered a novice in politics and the opposition used to make fun of him
 lekin ab vakt badal gaya he, wo congress ke adhyaksh ban chuke hai or party ko unase kaaphi ummiden hai
 Rahul's ascension to the post of president has looked very spectacular for the Congress so far
